  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ab8c7fbe-571c-46f4-9e85-d650975aa09f'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText2888093142610181166" style="display:none"><i>Librarian's note: An alternate cover edition can be found <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35006004.here" title="here" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a></i><br /><br />Their love had the power of a runaway freight train, and the potential to be just as destructive. <br />The tempestuous sequel to Bad Things picks up where the first book left off. Reeling from a profound loss, Tristan and Danika struggle to pick up the pieces and build a life together, but the hard habits of a lifetime are not so easy to escape. <br />Rock Bottom takes us on a dual point of view journey through addiction and desire, through love and agony, and answers the question we’ve been asking since these characters were introduced in Grounded: “What happened between Tristan and Danika?” <br /><br />DANIKA <br />Even love couldn’t cushion a fall like ours. My love for Tristan was so big that I felt consumed by it, and even so, it was not enough to overpower our combined demons. <br />I struggled. I yelled and screamed. I scratched and kicked. <br />I fought like hell, but even the most determined fighters have to stop before they break. <br />No one could say I didn’t fight for him. <br />“I love you,” I spoke softly into his ear. <br />He gripped me harder. “I can’t ever lose you, Danika. I’m not sure I’d survive it.” <br />“You’ve got me. And I’m not going anywhere. Not ever.” <br />I meant the words when I said them, but life had other plans for us. <br />I’d have given my life for that fight. In fact, I very nearly did. <br /><br />TRISTAN <br />She was the one. <br />If I’d ever had a doubt, I didn’t now. She was the one I’d be thinking about, longing for, until I took my last breath. If I lost her tomorrow, I’d pine for her like a lovesick fool. <br />This was the kind of love that only hit you once in your life. <br /><br />This book is intended for readers 18 and up.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14038642666565972959"><u>***THIS REVIEW CONTAINS SPOILERS.***</u><br/><br/>…What<br/><br/>…The<br/><br/>…Fuck<br/><br/><b>…HAPPENED?</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/giphy.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387743477ra/7661640.gif' alt=' photo giphy.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>To say that I was waiting for this book’s release is a VAST understatement. I mean, I love R.K. And we’re talking major-swooning here, okay? Especially with <b>Tristan and Danika’s</b> story because it’s been hinted at and hinted at <i>and hinted at</i>. And *FINALLY* I was going to find out what happened! <br/><br/>Well, I did.<br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/images3-1.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387743477i/7661641.jpg' alt=' photo images3-1.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>And I ain’t happy.</b><br/><br/>Sorry, <i>Rock Bottom</i> fans because…<br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_inline_mge9tqfXBU1rbumi6.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428573ra/857734.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_inline_mge9tqfXBU1rbumi6.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><u> --> PROBLEM #1 <-- </u><br/><br/>First off, I knew that it was going to be intense. A</span>
  <span id="freeText14038642666565972959" style="display:none"><u>***THIS REVIEW CONTAINS SPOILERS.***</u><br><br>…What<br><br>…The<br><br>…Fuck<br><br><b>…HAPPENED?</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/giphy.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387743477ra/7661640.gif" alt=" photo giphy.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>To say that I was waiting for this book’s release is a VAST understatement. I mean, I love R.K. And we’re talking major-swooning here, okay? Especially with <b>Tristan and Danika’s</b> story because it’s been hinted at and hinted at <i>and hinted at</i>. And *FINALLY* I was going to find out what happened! <br><br>Well, I did.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/images3-1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387743477i/7661641.jpg" alt=" photo images3-1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>And I ain’t happy.</b><br><br>Sorry, <i>Rock Bottom</i> fans because…<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_inline_mge9tqfXBU1rbumi6.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428573ra/857734.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mge9tqfXBU1rbumi6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><u> --&gt; PROBLEM #1 &lt;-- </u><br><br>First off, I knew that it was going to be intense. And emotional. And that I was probably going to spill my vodka on my Kindle because of the emotional trauma of the story. <b>I get that, okay?</b> <br>I was prepared! I was LOOKING FORWARD TO IT! But I think what the problem was is that I was kind of… I don’t know, expecting this huge and epic and powerful and severe *scene*. <br><br>And what I <i>got</i> was an entire book like that. <br><br><b>I wanted a train wreck and instead, I got a 20-car pileup.</b><br><br>Basically. <br><br><u> --&gt; PROBLEM #2 &lt;-- </u><br><br>Danika.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_lmss2ckKM81qgy5npo1_400.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387743477ra/7661642.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lmss2ckKM81qgy5npo1_400.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I think… that if Danika was blind, deaf, <i>and mute</i>; <b>she would have been an awesome character.</b><br><br>And that’s all I’m going to say about that. <br><br><b>So.</b><br><br><i>
  <u>Do I recommend this book?</u>
</i> YES. Because you do get to find out what happens. And you’ll need to read this one in order to read the third book. :)<br><br><i>
  <u>Do I still LOVE R.K.?</u>
</i> HELL YES! And I can’t wait for the next one!<br><br><i>
  <u>How steamy is this book on a scale of 1 to Christian Grey?</u>
</i> Eh. I’d give it a 4. It wasn’t that steamy at all, actually.<br><br><u>
  <b>
    <i>That’s all.</i>
  </b>
</u><br><br><i>This ARC was kindly provided and *very* happily received in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br><br><br></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_680397953" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/680397953" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/680397953?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer680397953" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10009721810903559163"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385321436i/7125659._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385245538ra/7106615.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> ** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ** </b><br/><br/>What an emotional roller coaster!!!<br/><br/><b>R.K. Lilley has a way of drawing you right into each book she writes and <i>Rock Bottom</i> tugged at every one of my heart strings. <br/><br/>Tristan and Danika's journey was emotional, intense, and heartbreaking but left me hopeful and eager for more. I absolutely adore this series and can't wait for the next book!! </b><br/><br/>Even before I started this book, I <em>knew</em> it was going to be an intense ride. This book picks up right where Book #1, <em>Bad Things</em>, ende</span>
  <span id="freeText10009721810903559163" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385321436i/7125659._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385245538ra/7106615.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> ** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ** </b><br><br>What an emotional roller coaster!!!<br><br><b>R.K. Lilley has a way of drawing you right into each book she writes and <i>Rock Bottom</i> tugged at every one of my heart strings. <br><br>Tristan and Danika's journey was emotional, intense, and heartbreaking but left me hopeful and eager for more. I absolutely adore this series and can't wait for the next book!! </b><br><br>Even before I started this book, I <em>knew</em> it was going to be an intense ride. This book picks up right where Book #1, <em>Bad Things</em>, ended and given what we knew of Tristan and Danika's relationship in the <em>Up In The Air</em> trilogy (see more info on the timeline below), we knew that they were going to go through some extreme heart ache. I had so many questions -- Where did Danika get her limp? What could possibly have happened to come between them??<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I love you," he rasped out. He said it all the time. He didn't hold it back, now that he'd admitted it, but it still gave me butterflies, every single time.</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"I love you," I spoke softly into his ear."</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>He gripped me harder. "I can't ever lose you, Danika. I'm not sure I'd survive it."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Well, <em>all</em> our questions were answered here. It was devastating to see a couple that was as powerfully in love with each other as Tristan and Danika facing so much pain but I loved the way the story was portrayed. It was told to us in alternating POVs and the thing I've always loved about both Tristan and Danika is that, while they each had their flaws, once you got inside their heads it was easy to at least <em>understand</em> where they were both coming from... even if at times I just wanted to shake them.<br><br>Danika's POV especially gave a lot of foreshadowing because it was written as though she'd already experienced all the events of this book and was almost looking back warning us of which little elements would come into play in a bigger way later on and impact their future. This really set a powerful tone of anticipation and dread. Honestly, there were times when I had to just put the book down for a few minutes and go watch a fluffy YouTube video or something just to calm down.<br><br>Ohhhh Tristan. My heart just went out to him. He was this totally badass guy with a serious saviour complex and an overprotective side that was in a constant state of overdrive. A true Alpha caveman if there ever was one. But he was also just a very flawed and tortured individual who'd suffered an extreme amount of loss and bore too much guilt on his shoulders. (And just as a side note, I really liked how the author included him being a rock star into the story without actually making this a "rock star story".)<br><br>I loved Danika too. She was sassy and feisty but also deeply caring and also damaged as well. But I loved how despite her insecurities, she relentlessly kept trying so hard to make things work.<br><br>My heart really broke for them both. They were so clearly in <em>love</em> with each other but life just kept throwing obstacle after obstacle at them. The more I read, the greater my dread grew. I <em>knew</em> something horrible was going to happen and my heart was already breaking. It was like a train wreck... I didn't want the inevitable to happen but was powerless to stop it.<br><br>Now... the #1 question: Does this book end on a cliffhanger?<br><br>The answer is both yes and no. At the end of this book, Tristan and Danika have reached their breaking point. They've been crushed by the events in their lives and are collectively paying the price of various wrong decisions. They are not "together" as a couple at the end but this actually fits perfectly into the timeline of the Up In The Air trilogy in which they are estranged.<br><br>However!!!! Before you run away.... there is a Teaser for Book #3 at the end which will leave you in a much better place. It shows the beginning of their reunion and is full of emotion and hope. I have a strong feeling that Book #3 is going to be all kinds of epic :)<br><br>You should also know that this book isn't only full of heartbreak. There's so much more to it. We see Tristan and Danika fall even deeper in love and share some absolutely beautiful, joyful times together.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"This is forever for me, sweetheart. I want it all with you. You're the thing that gets me up in the morning and lets me rest easy at night…"</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Ooooooh!!! Also, there was one scene from Frankie's POV in which we got to see James Cavendish five years before he met Bianca and all I have to say is OHHH. MY. GOD. !!!!!! *jaw drop* ;)<br><br>As an author, R.K. Lilley has really earned my trust. I love her writing style and I have consistently loved the direction that she's taken all her stories in and I fully trust that even though Tristan and Danika are at a low point now, that it'll make their reunion in the next book that much sweeter. <br><br>Tristan and Danika are the kind of couple who you just <em>know</em> are meant to be together. I can't wait to see them get their happily ever after!!<br><br>Rating: 4.5 stars (same rating as book #1)<br><br>*******************************<br><br><blockquote>
  <strong>TIMELINE CLARIFICATION</strong>
</blockquote><br><br>The <em>Tristan &amp; Danika</em> trilogy is a spin-off of the <em>Up In The Air </em>trilogy (in which we first met Tristan and Danika as side characters). Both trilogies can be read on their own though and you don't <em>need</em> to read them both to understand the stories. However, their timelines are interconnected.<br><br>The first 2 books of this trilogy, <em>Bad</em> <em>Things</em> and <em>Rock</em> <em>Bottom</em> take place 5 years before <em>In</em> <em>Flight</em> (the first book in the <em>Up In The Air </em>trilogy). Then, chronologically, come the three books of the <em>Up In The Air</em> trilogy.... and then finally comes <em>Lovely Trigger</em> (the last book in the <em>Tristan &amp; Danika</em> trilogy).<br><br>Anyone who has read the <em>Up In The Air</em> trilogy will know that during the course of those books, Tristan and Danika had an estranged and strained relationship but what we didn't know was <em>why. </em>We saw Tristan and Danika fall in love in <em>Bad Things</em>, then in <em>Rock</em> <em>Bottom</em> we learned the full reason for their estrangement, which then perfectly set up the final book, <em>Lovely</em> <em>Trigger</em> which will be a second-chance romance.<br><br>So chronologically, this would be the order of the books:<br><br>✦ Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika #1)<br>✦ Rock Bottom (Tristan &amp; Danika #2) - <em>starts right after Bad Things</em><br>✦ In Flight (Up In The Air #1) - <em>starts 5 years after the end of Rock Bottom</em><br>✦ Mile High (Up In The Air #2)<br>✦ Grounded (Up In The Air #3)<br>✦ Lovely Trigger (Tristan &amp; Danika #3) - <em>starts </em><i>6 years after the end of Rock Bottom </i><br><br>However, the suggested reading order is to read all 3 <em>Up In The Air</em> books, and then the <em>Tristan &amp; Danika</em> trilogy. Trust me, it all works out very clearly :)<br><br>*Lovely Trigger is expected to release early 2014.<br><br>*******************************<br><br>This is my casting for Tristan:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410623i/805391.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10009721810903559163" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText5387167617089935825" style="display:none">It's live!! &gt;&gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1gGSqRo">http://amzn.to/1gGSqRo</a> &lt;&lt;<br><br><b>6 EMOTIONALLY DEVASTATING ~ HEARTWRENCHING ~ BEAUTIFULLY BROKEN STARS!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385421690i/7145695._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385421690i/7145696.jpg" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>.....they sure did. But was it enough?<br><br><b>Cheating?</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No, not emotionally. When they are <i>together</i>, definitely no form of physical or emotional cheating takes place, though lots of groupies try. When, um, they’re going through...rough patches...there may be a scene...near the end...where something...physical...takes place *voice cracks* <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Cliffhanger?</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes and No. <i>Definitely</i> leaves you wanting more, DEFINITELY! The ending of this book just about tore me apart, <b><i>but</i></b> R.K. was kind enough to include a sneak peek into book 3 that will definitely be a small salve. Still not enough though, just sayin’. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Don't try to prepare yourself for this rollercoaster and post gifs saying your body is ready. Cuz it ain't.<br><br>So a quick breakdown:<br><br><b>Hot, kinky sex?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/650962.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Possessive, protective, caveman hero?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/650962.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Sweet, compassionate, feisty, strong-willed heroine?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/650962.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>A twist you’ll never see coming?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/650962.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Relationship cracks?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/650962.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Reaches relationship breaking point?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/650962.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Terrible, horrible, scared-to-flip-the-page event?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/650962.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cry your eyeballs out?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/650962.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>But I loved it anyway?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/650962.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So did you get the story? *laugh*<br><br><b>*Here<br><br>It*<br><br>*Begins</b><br><br>This book picks up right after the events of Bad Things, and though I was ecstatic and elated to see their relationship grow, I also had this pit in my stomach because of what would occur later. If you’ve read the Up in the Air series, you know that Danika and Tristan are separated then, and Danika has a physical deformity. My biggest question I wanted an answer to, but at the same time I didn’t, was <i>
  <b>where did she get that limp from?</b>
</i><br><br>Rest assured, the answer to that question and so many others are all revealed here. I want to say first though, R.K. Lilley has a way, no, a talent for sucking you right into the story with her addictive writing style. I mean, I’ve never read a book so fast nor have I forgotten to pee (TMI? Sorry). I was already convinced of her work with the Up in the Air trilogy, but this series?? <u>Completely</u> knocks James and Bianca <b>out.of.the.ballpark.</b> I honestly think this spinoff is her best work to date (all of her books are fab) and Rock Bottom is by far my favorite. <br><br>Back to the book. Now that Tristan and Danika are “settled” into their relationship, it was extremely heartwarming to see their love for each other blossom even more, despite so many obstacles that try to trip them up. Tristan’s mother, Danika’s mother, Tristan’s alcoholism, Danika’s sister, Tristan’s temper, etc…the list keeps going. Yet it never stops them. They learn to divide and conquer, one step at a time. And at the same time, their love for each other only intensifies in magnitude. <br><br><b>
  <i>“She was the one. If I’d ever had a doubt, I didn’t now. She was the one I’d be thinking about, longing for, until I took my last breath. If I lost her tomorrow, I’d pine for her like a lovesick fool. This was the kind of love that only hit you once in your life.”</i>
</b><br><br>Which made my heart shatter even more when I started to see cracks in their foundation. Nothing big at first, just little kinks here and there. Late night out partying, too much classwork, practicing with the band, dancing in the studio. Jealousy. Alcoholism. Groupies. Little by little, these tiny pieces built up into something explosive, until they turned the blame on each other.<br><br><b>
  <i>“There was an anchor, tied around both of his ankles, and it was taking him deep, into black fathomless depths, drowning him slowly but surely.”<br><br>“I didn’t tell him that he was dragging me down with him.”</i>
</b><br><br>At one point, I actually just wanted them to call quits to their relationship. This couple was dysfunctional, their love starting to turn into poison in their blood. But then, it would get better. They truly are each other’s crutch and kryptonite, needing each other so, but each having the power to destroy the other.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I can’t ever lose you, Danika. I’m not sure I’d survive it.”<br><br>“You’ve got me. And I’m not going anywhere. Not ever.”</i>
</b><br><br>Why can’t love ever be simple? Why must it be corrupted by outside forces that only serve to tear them apart? Why, why, why, why?<br><br><b>*And<br><br>The*<br><br><i>Thing*</i><br><br>*Happens</b><br><br>It was a trainwreck I couldn’t take my eyes off of, wanting to stop it, but helpless to do so. It was an execution, only in slow motion so that they took the full brunt of the force. You could’ve thrust a dagger in my side and it would’ve been less painful than to read about the disastrous, shocking events that <i>
  <b>ripped</b>
</i> the couple apart. Not just their couple status. <b>Ripped.<i>Them</i>.Apart.</b><br><br>I cried.<br><br><b>I cried some more.</b><br><br>I kept crying.<br><br><b>I cried even more</b><br><br>I couldn’t stop crying.<br><br><b>And then I went to go put on extra mascara because it was time for work.</b><br><br>As you already know, the ending devastated me, but only R.K. Lilley could weave such a story and get away with it without me hunting her down (JK!!). Just barely, by the way. If you looked at the spoiler tag in the beginning of the review, you'll see that the ending leaves you anticipating the events in book 3 (like their reunion ASAP!!!) so I'm not <i>that</i> worried. Okay. Maybe I am. But I'm just a natural worrier. Counting down the days for Lovely Trigger!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="5387167617089935825" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_639237272" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639237272" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/639237272?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer639237272" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18019720828381894461"><b>5 Painful Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/b82e2380-e897-41e3-9475-fbea9a13fea0_zps6d6e07d8.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385977499i/7268122.jpg' alt='Rock Bottom photo b82e2380-e897-41e3-9475-fbea9a13fea0_zps6d6e07d8.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <blockquote>Their love had the power of a runaway freight train, and the potential to be just as destructive.</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>I loved this book, but it was devastating to read. It’s taken me an entire week to write this review. It was such a great sequel, but it seriously hurt. I’m talking rip your heart out, uncontrollable sobbing kind of hurt. There was an intensity there- even though I knew it would be intense and emotional, it put me through the ringer. Anyone who has read the Up In the Air tri</span>
  <span id="freeText18019720828381894461" style="display:none"><b>5 Painful Stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/b82e2380-e897-41e3-9475-fbea9a13fea0_zps6d6e07d8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385977499i/7268122.jpg" alt="Rock Bottom photo b82e2380-e897-41e3-9475-fbea9a13fea0_zps6d6e07d8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>Their love had the power of a runaway freight train, and the potential to be just as destructive.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I loved this book, but it was devastating to read. It’s taken me an entire week to write this review. It was such a great sequel, but it seriously hurt. I’m talking rip your heart out, uncontrollable sobbing kind of hurt. There was an intensity there- even though I knew it would be intense and emotional, it put me through the ringer. Anyone who has read the Up In the Air trilogy and Bad Things, you had questions. Well, happy to say all questions have been answered. You get to see all the events that led up to where Tristan and Danika have ended up. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/be967eef-1004-4dfa-b834-666d42641b9b_zpsdb66750c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385977499i/7268123.jpg" alt="Rock Bottom photo be967eef-1004-4dfa-b834-666d42641b9b_zpsdb66750c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Rock Bottom starts right where Bad Things leaves off. Tristan and Danika are both still grieving their loss. It’s hard on them both, but they are trying to get through it together. They need each other. Tristan can’t survive without Danika. He’s lost most everything thats important to him. He can’t lose her. Not ever. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/ee35fb4d-6551-4c5c-a7d0-cb013d797a45_zps3a51dca3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385977499i/7268124.jpg" alt="Rock Bottom photo ee35fb4d-6551-4c5c-a7d0-cb013d797a45_zps3a51dca3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I don’t want to go much into the story. It is one you should read for yourself and would be a huge disservice to spoil anything. I will talk about the characters- Tristan and Danika.<br><br><b>Tristan</b>- My beautiful broken man... Tristan takes my love for damaged guys to a whole other level. Tristan has so many demons. All the loss he endured, he coped with it the only way he knew how. I love his protective, possessive, caveman alpha side. He also had a sweet and caring side. He truly loves Danika, but he doesn’t always handle things with her the way he should. <br><br><b>Danika</b>- How much devastation and loss should one person be forced to bear? Her story was brutal. Seriously brutal. She loves Tristan, she loves him unconditionally, but she also enables him. She tried so hard to fight for him and their relationship. Even with her enabling him, she had her moments where her spunky and feisty personality shined through. <br><br><br>Tristan and Danika’s love is all consuming. Nothing could ever tear them apart. Or so they think. Death. Drugs. Alcohol. Loss. Destruction. Everything spiraling out of control...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/32838265-e937-43cd-a491-7ee5a27111c6_zps8b70cc0a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385977499i/7268125.jpg" alt="Rock Bottom photo 32838265-e937-43cd-a491-7ee5a27111c6_zps8b70cc0a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What will happen when this couple hits their rock bottom? Will they survive it together, intact? Or will everything they’ve built crumble.... <br><br>Tristan and Danika have been through more loss and heartbreak than any two people should ever have to go through. My heart ached for the both of them. This book was so hard to read. I didn’t want to put it down, yet I had trouble continuing after certain scenes. It will draw you in, captivate you. R.K. Lilley is a fantastic writer, her books just have a flow to them. I just want to say how grateful I am that there was a chapter/sneak peek from the third book at the end. Without that, it would have been so much harder to deal with the ending. As sad as it was, there was a lot of beauty, a lot of steam, and even some humor. So even though I cried my eyes out, that wasn’t the entire part of the book. I cannot wait for the third and final installment to come out, early 2014! I need these two to have the ending that they deserve. This is an amazing series you don’t want to miss out on! <br><b>
  <blockquote>Tragedy never took its full chunk out of you right way. It always took a while to hit you head on, and sink in and for something substantial, some hint of the real feeling, the real reaction, to come to the surface, and this loss was not done taking its toll on us. </blockquote>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/6d950c73-143b-432f-a642-ac5fd2531684_zpsc4162fce.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385977500i/7268126.jpg" alt="Rock Bottom photo 6d950c73-143b-432f-a642-ac5fd2531684_zpsc4162fce.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i> “I have many regrets, many bad things I must take credit for, but believe me when I say that the negative impact that all of my actions have had on your life is my biggest one.”</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="18019720828381894461" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_639534032" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639534032" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/639534032?book_show_action=true">Jun 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13126896-michelle?shelf=01-signed">01-signed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer639534032" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9438124700448284975"><b>5+ OHMYGODMYHEARTHURTS stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385451635i/7151007.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>We were introduced to Danika and Tristan during R.K. Lilley’s Up In The Air Series. We knew they once loved each other; that a tragedy tore them apart, and for the first time we are going to learn the truth. <i>
  <b>How a two people’s past can be the most heartbreaking and breathtaking moments of their lives. </b>
</i> <br/><br/>Rock Bottom begins just were Bad Things ended. Danika is the life preserver that Tristan is clinging to. She is the only thing giving his life breath. The time aft</span>
  <span id="freeText9438124700448284975" style="display:none"><b>5+ OHMYGODMYHEARTHURTS stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385451635i/7151007.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>We were introduced to Danika and Tristan during R.K. Lilley’s Up In The Air Series. We knew they once loved each other; that a tragedy tore them apart, and for the first time we are going to learn the truth. <i>
  <b>How a two people’s past can be the most heartbreaking and breathtaking moments of their lives. </b>
</i> <br><br>Rock Bottom begins just were Bad Things ended. Danika is the life preserver that Tristan is clinging to. She is the only thing giving his life breath. The time after Jared’s death are the moments where they can protect their love from destruction. But life continues on and staying swept up in each other’s arms ignoring the world around them isn't going to magically make the grief disappear. <br><br><i>The outside world is just waiting for the moment to come crashing down, testing them, testing just how much love can endure before it’s just not enough.</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “Every misstep that led us down the path to our destruction was our own doing, but to this day, I still hated that guitar.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385451635i/7151008.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>This is the story of what tore Tristan &amp; Danika apart. <br>The missing pieces. <br>The part of the story where we learn the answers to the questions. <br>And this is the part of the story that will fracture our hearts as we watch them shatter.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385451635i/7151009.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>The reconstruction of Tristan &amp; Danika’s story was one of the hardest things I've endured as a reader. Learning how they fell in love and how deeply they loved, knowing that they did not make it and having to watch that unfold was utterly heartbreaking. </i><br><br>This was not just about what unraveled and what ultimately broke two people who loved so deeply. This was about the fight to save the one person you would give your life for and facing the reality of having to let go to save yourself. A complete emotional breakdown kind of read. Danika’s urge to enable and Tristan’s demons that had him in a death grip. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “I lay down on my bed and did not get back up.<br>Not for hours.<br>Not for days.<br>What was left of a woman when she gave a man everything?<br>The answer was easy.<br>Impossible to deny, even for me.<br>Nothing.<br>Had I given too much? Was there enough of me left to even try to move on from this?”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I think I felt my first tear drop around the 70% mark and by the time I reached the end I was a complete mess. There are eye opening moments that I never even imagined being brought into the story-line, making it ultimately that much more heartbreaking. <br><br>Tristan’s constant struggle with his own demons was hard to read, Danika’s constant need to appease his behavior did not annoy me as I expected. It saddened me. R.K. Lilley did a brilliant job creating the abuser/enabler relationship between these two, often a side to a story that is hard to relate to without experiencing it personally. <br><br>R.K. Lilley absolutely amazed me with the way she told their story. I am so pleased that she decided to take this two book series and turn it into a trilogy. You see, although Rock Bottom untangles the mystery of what we saw in Grounded, it in no way completes the story. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385451635i/7151010.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>We are taken back to the very first hello and led to the very last goodbye. We are not given closure. </b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “He was too callous, too far gone to realize that I’d never be free of him, and that he’d really done was set me adrift. I never left that bed.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Now, some may call this a cliffhanger… I’m not sold on that concept. Lovely Trigger will pick up in present time and will be the conclusion of their story. <b> A story that will be read by us, knowing the highs and the lows and allowing us to watch what I hope is a devastatingly beautiful second chance at love. </b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="9438124700448284975" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer701415906" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9030148828297537492"><b>4 Gut-Wrenching Stars</b><br/><br/>I waited until book three was released before starting this story and, boy, am I glad I did. This book gutted me and left me with very mixed emotions. I loved it and hated it equally. The drama became over-the-top, gut-wrenching, and too much for one couple to find their way to a believable, albeit eventual HEA. Still, I never felt like abandoning the story. In fact, quite the opposite; I couldn't put it down. I have never read a romance couple that has intrigued me or captu</span>
  <span id="freeText9030148828297537492" style="display:none"><b>4 Gut-Wrenching Stars</b><br /><br />I waited until book three was released before starting this story and, boy, am I glad I did. This book gutted me and left me with very mixed emotions. I loved it and hated it equally. The drama became over-the-top, gut-wrenching, and too much for one couple to find their way to a believable, albeit eventual HEA. Still, I never felt like abandoning the story. In fact, quite the opposite; I couldn't put it down. I have never read a romance couple that has intrigued me or captured my attention quite like Tristan and Danika have. I really hope the author can make me a believer of their eventual HEA in book three. <br /><br />Now, off to read book three. Eek! <br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>September 15, 2013 Pre-Review Comment</u>
</b> <br /><br />I was very disheartened to find out this couple's story WILL NOT end with this book like originally planned. It makes me sad I'll have to wait until book three (and pay more money) to get Tristan and Danika's HEA. I'm tired of romance trilogies! </span>
  <a data-text-id="9030148828297537492" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_681425839" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/681425839" />
    <a title="Mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22667925-mia"><img alt="Mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406604077p2/22667925.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/681425839?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mia" href="/user/show/22667925-mia">Mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22667925-mia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer681425839" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11810211949601662579">This book was a <b><br/>HEART BREAKING, <br/>GUT WRENCHING, <br/>SOUL ACHING, <br/>EMOTIONAL TRAIN WRECK.</b><br/><br/>Reading the book:<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/648861.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The end:<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403256ra/784470.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Finishing the book:<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385944928ra/7263367.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“There was an anchor, tied around both of his ankles, and it was taking him deep, into black fathomless depths, drowning him slowly but surely. I didn’t tell him that he was dragging me down with him.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>I think what made this book 100 times harder to read was the fact that we all knew something bad was coming. Along with the clever way the author wrote this book</span>
  <span id="freeText11810211949601662579" style="display:none">This book was a <b><br>HEART BREAKING, <br>GUT WRENCHING, <br>SOUL ACHING, <br>EMOTIONAL TRAIN WRECK.</b><br><br>Reading the book:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/648861.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The end:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403256ra/784470.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Finishing the book:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385944928ra/7263367.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“There was an anchor, tied around both of his ankles, and it was taking him deep, into black fathomless depths, drowning him slowly but surely. I didn’t tell him that he was dragging me down with him.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>I think what made this book 100 times harder to read was the fact that we all knew something bad was coming. Along with the clever way the author wrote this book in past tense, with little monologues at the end of chapters, the sense of dread that fills you while reading this book was like a full grown elephant sitting on your chest. <b>Hindsight is a bitch.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“She smiled that smile where I saw myself and forever in her eyes, and gave me everything. She was selfless, my Danika, keeping nothing for herself.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Tristan and Danika are one of my all-time favourite book couples. To this day, they hold the number one spot for the best chemistry on my book shelves. Reading the first book, I couldn’t help but thing how <b>good</b> they are together, no matter how dysfunctional, they are meant to be! <br><br>In every way that the first book was witty, light, sweet and sexy, this book was the complete opposite. It broke my heart with every page and it was so hard seeing characters that I loved so much, become so <b>bad</b> for each other. The first half of the book was mostly slowbuiling tension between the two and they dealt with insecurities and trying to maintain a doomed long distance relationship. Slowly but surely, their relationship just became so unhealthy. At so many times I just wanted to shake them both! It was hardest watching Tristan, a character I love and feel so invested in, deal with so many problems: depression, self-hatred, and his addiction. Danika became the one thing she swore she'd never come back to —she became his enabler. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“She was the one. If I’d ever had a doubt, I didn’t now. She was the one I’d be thinking about, longing for, until I took my last breath. If I lost her tomorrow, I’d pine for her like a lovesick fool. This was the kind of love that only hit you once in your life.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>With the little titbits of their story we got from grounded, I assumed that the worst that happened to Danika and Tristan was probably just some drunk driving incident… boy was I wrong. This book absolutely GUTTED me. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[First Tristan's brother died, than his mom, a miscarriage, a marriage and a divorce, an almost-rape, a crazy-dean car accident, ANOTHER misscarrage, and Danika never being able to dance again or have kids <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>… clearly RK Lilley had no mercy for our beloved Danika and Tristan. it was brutal, absolutely brutal.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You’ve got me. And I’m not going anywhere. Not ever.” <br>I meant the words when I said them, but life had other plans for us. <br>I’d have given my life for that fight. In fact, I very nearly did.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Reading this book a second time made me appreciate the writing even more! The way RK Lilley wrote this book was pure freaking genius. It was written in past tense, but not just using past participles... It's hard to explain because there really were no flash backs. The entire book takes place 'in the moment' but the author would end chapters with short monologues or put little comments here and there within Danika and Tristan's thoughts that made you feel like they're telling their story from another time or another place. An example was this scene that absolutely tore my heart out and ripped it in two:<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<blockquote><i>“I never left that bed.<br>That feeling of helpless abandonment and unendurable longing stayed inside of me, for hours, for months, for minutes, for weeks. <br><b>For years. <br>I went through my life, through tragedy and pain, through hardship and life, and my heart, my very soul, stayed in that bed. <br>I felt broken after that last encounter. <br>Was broken. </b><br>Pieces of me had been shattered on that bed, important, essential pieces, and they would not, could not, ever find their way back together.”</i></blockquote>
<br>^^That makes much more sense now, knowing that lovely trigger will take place 6 years later! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>All said and done, it was an amazing book. It was so well written and fiercely emotional. I was torn between finishing the book as fast as I could and never wanting to read the ending. RK Lilley still holds her spot as one of my favourite authors and I think it was a very smart move turning this series into a trilogy. With the readers having seen every aspect of Danika and Tristan's relationship, Lovely Trigger will be a whirl wind of emotions. <br><br>THANK GOD for that teaser (which I have already read, re-read and cried over a good 10 times) at the end because I have no clue how I'd get through the next few months without having that to hold on to... I CANNOT WAIT to get my hands on Lovely Trigger. I look forward to seeing where Danika and Tristan are in 6 years and seeing them get the HEA they deserve!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394303557i/8833543._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><a>Book 1 review</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/743538479?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Book 3 review</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="11810211949601662579" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

</p><p><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387691918ra/7652446.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><b>I understood his conflicted and tortured feelings but the way he handled them was all wrong. That's all I'm going to say about that. I still liked him most of the time though and well, his possessive streak makes him:</b></p><p>

  <br/>
  <b>BUT a lot of trouble could have been avoi</b></p></span>
  <span id="freeText13708061333572644708" style="display:none">★★★★ <b>4 'Rock Bottom' stars!<br><br>Whew, this book was devastatingly tragic, especially the last 30% of the story and it left me feeling a little like this...</b><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380436052ra/881173.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393960701ra/8787770.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>First of all, Tristan:</b>
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394803008ra/8908116.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387691918ra/7652446.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><b>I understood his conflicted and tortured feelings but the way he handled them was all wrong. That's all I'm going to say about that. I still liked him most of the time though and well, his possessive streak makes him:</b></p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390285357ra/8183974.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>And then there's Danika...</b>
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393689103ra/8752543.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <b>BUT a lot of trouble could have been avoided if T &amp; D would have just communicated a bit more instead of keeping so many secrets.</b>
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385781618ra/7226595.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>To Twatalie and Dean:</b>

  <br>
  <i>Except for those few random scenes told in her POV, she was a fun character and a great addition to the story.</i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>Despite all the angst, or maybe even because of it, this was still a highly enjoyable, captivating read and if you haven't read this series yet, do yourself a favor and give it a try! Now I'm off to the final chapter of this story!</b>

  <span id="freeText9654423131650304740" style="display:none"><b>"Heart in tatters, but will intact, I went on with my life."</b> <br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/Kingsleyfragile.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/649611.gif" alt=" photo slowclap.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>To sum up Danika &amp; Tristan's second installment I think the following gif does it nicely... <br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/reality.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385693755ra/7203127.gif" alt=" photo reality.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>That was pretty much the entire book. I knew that it was going to be a really difficult read and I knew I was going to need tissues and be upset but I had no idea just how heart breaking it would all be. By the time I got to the last 15 or 20 percent of the book I wasn't sure if I was going to make it or not. This was absolutely fantastically done. I'm also so very thankful that she put the first chapter of the next book at the end. It helped bring me out of that time frame and back to the nearer present. I will say that R.K. apparently has a knack for being able to rip your heart out and crush it while you're still alive and do it in a way that you can keep reading. I definitely did not read it as quickly as I could have, but I could not put it down either. Every tragedy was a train wreck and I could not look away for even a second. I am going to have to stick to the lighter side of things for the next few books just to get over this one. I'm glad Lovely Trigger is out early 2014... I am absolutely eager to see where this story goes. <br><br>FUCKING FANTASTIC!!!! <br><br></span>

  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br/><br/>Beware!! this book is one HUGE train wreck after another.....<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385480920ra/7159048.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>but we all knew <i>it had to be!!</i> And I definitely agree with having three books. <br/><br/>So, let's break things down...<br/><br/><br/><b>The Good:</b><br/><br/>✦ The sex....<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380297835i/682354.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>"I" even got shivers when Tristan would say <b>

  <span id="freeText17429666207763491653" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br><br>Beware!! this book is one HUGE train wreck after another.....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385480920ra/7159048.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>but we all knew <i>it had to be!!</i> And I definitely agree with having three books. <br><br>So, let's break things down...<br><br><br><b>The Good:</b><br><br>✦ The sex....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380297835i/682354.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>"I" even got shivers when Tristan would say <b>
  <i>"Ride me."</i>
</b><br><br>✦ Frankie - I loved her with Danika but... (*check the "ugly" section for more*)<br><br>✦ Bev!! I never warmed up to her much before but she stole the show in this book!<br><br>✦ Sakura from Naruto - that was hilarious!<br><br>✦ Dual POVs! love that!<br><br>✦ The weekend getaways especially the one! I loved Danika's reaction in the restaurant!<br><br><br><b>The Bad:</b><br><br>✦ Dean...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384017732ra/6747642.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Karma, baby! But, I need answers! <i>(and he definitely fits under "ugly" too!)</i><br><br>✦ Twatalie...that was disappointing! Even though she's disgusting, there could've been some good drama there.<br><br>✦ Marta (Danika's mom) and Bert. 'Nuff said.<br><br>✦ Dahlia...I'm lumping her into the "bad" section but I was worried several times that things could turn ugly. That being said, I think things are improving.<br><br>✦ "Boo" - just no. <br><br>✦ "Yanno" - just stop.<br><br>✦ Bronson Giles - will anything come out of that?<br><br>✦ What happened to the letter?<br><br><br><b>The Ugly:</b><br><br>You sure you want it? because...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385494017ra/7161269.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>it's rough, baby, <i>rough!</i><br><br><br>Well, let's get to it...<br><br>✦ The groupies...especially the last two although I must say it could've been much worse! It did make me feel better about Tristan's reaction. <br><br>✦ The drinking and the drugs...never a good thing.<br><br>✦ The distance just added to the toxic cocktail.<br><br>✦ Danika having to go through that TWO times was horrible. That alone would be enough to take down anyone but the part about the picture...ugh!<br><br>✦ Leticia...why not add more things?<br><br>✦ The ending part with Dean...I know this sounds bad but I much rather have that happen than what he planned.<br><br><i>* While these fit in the "ugly" category, they are also "WTF?" *</i><br><br>✦ The Frankie chapters...WTF were those about? And I need some eye bleach after reading the scenes with James...did we really need those? <br><br>✦ The Epilogue...the part with Tristan killed me.<br><br>✦ The Crossover bonus scene...??? I guess we'll get answers later.<br><br><br><b>Final Thoughts:</b><br><br>This book is depressing and I felt like it had to be but...it was a little too much. How much can two people take and survive? How much can a relationship take and recover? After reading the excerpt for <i>Lovely Trigger</i>, I have some concerns. I don't want things to get fixed too easily!<br><br><br><b>Thanks Melissa for the buddy read!!</b><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/630639.gif" width="400" height="050" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Favorite quotes:</b><br><br>❥ "This is all yours right here. All of me. No one else gets a thing from me, you understand? I wouldn’t do that to you. I wouldn’t make all these promises if I didn’t intend to keep them.”<br><br>❥ “Two cops Tasered me at the same time once, and it barely phased me.”<br><br>❥ “Everything you promised, and everything I need. What I’m willing to give to you is what I want from you. Can’t you do that for me, Tristan? Isn’t there enough of you left?” <br><br>❥ "My dear, this is what's called family."<br><br>❥ “I have many regrets, many bad things I must take credit for, but believe me when I say that the negative impact that all of my actions have had on your life is my biggest one.”</span>

<div id="review_742232696" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/742232696" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/742232696?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer742232696" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8273979368064930270"><b>4 (Dysfunctional Relationship) Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Rock Bottom is a ROCKY, CRAZY, You-Do-Not-Know-What-To-Expect Ride</b><br/><br/>Danika and Tristan are moving forward in their relationship. Tristan is taking Jared’s death as best as he can and luckily he has Danika to lean on. Tristan decides to rejoin the band and the band lands a record deal which brings Tristan to stay in LA five days of the week.<br/><br/>Danika can see slight changes in Tristan, but is so consumed by love, she’s coping as best as she can.<br/><br/> <b>Thoughts….Feelings…Em</b></span>
  <span id="freeText8273979368064930270" style="display:none"><b>4 (Dysfunctional Relationship) Stars</b><br><br><b>Rock Bottom is a ROCKY, CRAZY, You-Do-Not-Know-What-To-Expect Ride</b><br><br>Danika and Tristan are moving forward in their relationship. Tristan is taking Jared’s death as best as he can and luckily he has Danika to lean on. Tristan decides to rejoin the band and the band lands a record deal which brings Tristan to stay in LA five days of the week.<br><br>Danika can see slight changes in Tristan, but is so consumed by love, she’s coping as best as she can.<br><br> <b>Thoughts….Feelings…Emotions</b><br><br>Rock Bottom is EMOTIONAL. Be mentally prepared. I would almost say it mirrors the tension and angst of the Breaking Nova series by Jessica Sorensen. There is something about the way Lilley writes where she creates a couple that is just so raw, gritty and destructive, you can’t help, but love and cringe at the same time.<br><br>As much as I hate couples being separated in book 2 of series, Lilley did it the right way. There was hardly a separation, meaning, she wrote it when they were together, even though Tristan was away a good portion of the week. <br><br>In the beginning you can see Tristan internally struggle with Jared’s death and I would even say that Tristan and Danika kind of used their love and sex as a crutch to not deal with it. What I love most about the Tristan and Danika’s relationship is their intensity. Tristan takes the relationship to another level. I love his cave-man ways and reactions. Yes, many times Tristan reacts over the top by getting super jealous if Danika speaks to another guy, but to me, it made me fall in love with him more. <br><br> I love a damaged heroes and I knew Rock Bottom wouldn’t be an easy read. As Tristan stays in LA, over time, his period of stay is longer and he starts to change. It’s no surprise because his band mate, Dane is kind of bad influence and instigates a lot of issues. <br><br>As much as angsty this book was for me and as much as I do not like angst, there weren’t any annoying or frustrating moments. Yes, Tristan was out of control and sometimes Danika’s reactions weren’t agreeable, but to me, it just made me like the story more.<br><br>Also, there are no obvious moments. To me, I never knew what would happen next. Just when I think Lilley is setting up for a typical issue, she blows my mind and turns it into something else. I was shocked at the 50, 70, 90 and 99 percent mark. Crazy right?<br><br>I think I really enjoyed this book a lot because how crazy, messed-up, intense love Tristan and Danika have for each other. It was a yummy journey.<br><br>Is there HEA? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Is there a cliffy? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[YES! Be prepared to jump into book 3, Lovely Trigger ASAP <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/Lbe6rql" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413543i/814418.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Series Order</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17377032.Bad_Things__Tristan___Danika___1_" title="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1371404883s/17377032.jpg" alt="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/562175170" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00CX3F2QY/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00CX3F2QY&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18943009.Rock_Bottom__Tristan___Danika___2_" title="Rock Bottom (Tristan &amp; Danika, #2) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1385363364s/18943009.jpg" alt="Rock Bottom (Tristan &amp; Danika, #2) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00GW9K8EG/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00GW9K8EG&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><br>For more reviews, <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com">http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/a86FlrT" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381885730i/5378216._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385584721i/7179662.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was definitely worth the wait!<br>From the first time we started reading the Inflight series we were looking for answers...<br><br>What happened to Tristan <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385584721i/7179663.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and <br><br>Danika?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385584721i/7179664.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Why does she have a limp?<br><br>Why does she hate Tristan?<br><br>Does she even hate him?<br><br>So many questions, finally...<br>We get answers.<br><br>Now we know that Tristan and Danika have one of those forever loves: <br>Passionate, intense and all consuming....<br><br>Their love is like a drug. Tristan is still battling with his loss and only Danika can fill the void in his heart. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385584721i/7179665.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When an opportunity strikes Tristan and his band he is forced to make a decision, one that he didn't know would effect so many lives.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385584721i/7179666.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And this is the beginning of the end.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385584721i/7179667.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Some parts are painfully hard and sad to read and I don't blame Danika for feeling this way in the end.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385584721i/7179668.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I cannot wait for the next installment in this series because when you have that forever kind of love, you will never find anything which comes close to it and it's worth the wait and worth fighting for!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385584721i/7179669.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/639752108?book_show_action=true">Jun 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=cliffhanger">cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=erotic">erotic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=tissues-needed">tissues-needed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-alpha-hero">favorite-alpha-hero</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=continuing-plot">continuing-plot</a>,
