    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer639752108" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9153057226422331314"><b>5 Devastating Stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394579581i/8874109._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>There was an anchor, tied around both of his ankles, and it was taking him deep, into black fathomless depths, drowning him slowly but surely.   <br/><br/>I didn’t tell him that he was dragging me down with him.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434595ra/877296.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/>Sweet mother of angst. <b>THIS BOOK.</b> Gah! This fucking book. I knew it was coming. I prepared myself...at least I thought I did. But nothing, I mean nothing could have prepared me for the full emotional roller coaster that was the last 40% of this book. I can tell you</span>
  <span id="freeText9153057226422331314" style="display:none"><b>5 Devastating Stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394579581i/8874109._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">There was an anchor, tied around both of his ankles, and it was taking him deep, into black fathomless depths, drowning him slowly but surely.   <br><br>I didn’t tell him that he was dragging me down with him.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434595ra/877296.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Sweet mother of angst. <b>THIS BOOK.</b> Gah! This fucking book. I knew it was coming. I prepared myself...at least I thought I did. But nothing, I mean nothing could have prepared me for the full emotional roller coaster that was the last 40% of this book. I can tell you one thing; thank FUCK I waited for book 3 to be out to finally read this, because I'm pretty sure I would have gone from batshit straight into crazyville after that ending. <br><blockquote>
  <b>Their love had the power of a runaway freight train, and the potential to be just as destructive.</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394573081ra/8873278.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Rock Bottom starts where Bad Things left off; Tristan and Danika are dealing with the grief after Tristan's brother died. They both have their own demons that they're fighting, but they're fighting them together. You can feel the connection that they have through the pages. You want so bad for them to be happy and be okay, but in the back of your mind you know that there's a darkness that's looming over their relationship. You know it's coming, you know it will be bad, but you have no idea when. I swear, I think I was holding my breath in anticipation through the whole book.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I love you," I spoke softly into his ear.   <br>He gripped me harder. "I can’t ever lose you, Danika. I’m not sure I’d survive it."   <br>"You’ve got me.  And I’m not going anywhere. Not ever."   <br><br>I meant the words when I said them, but life had other plans for us.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380924018ra/3298476.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The odds were stacked against them from the beginning and as much as you're dreading for that moment to come, you know it's inevitable. I think that's what made this book so good, in a sadistic sort of way. That anticipation of not <b>if</b> but <b>when.</b><br><br>Slowly you see Tristan spiral out of control more and more. Danika tries to help him, and your heart breaks along with her watching him sink deeper and deeper into darkness.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Even love couldn’t cushion a fall like ours. My love for Tristan was so big that I felt consumed by it, and even so, it was not enough to overpower our combined demons.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394665176ra/8885766.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I finished this in one sitting. I simply couldn't put it down. I knew that whatever goes down between them is going to be bad. I just don't think I was prepared for just how bad it would be. My god! That ending! Everything that happens! Danika! Tristan! Gah!!<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <br>
  <blockquote>
    <b>
      <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Know that I would take it all back if I could, and know that I hold myself responsible for all of the bad things that happened. I am so sorry that my hitting rock bottom the way I did impacted you. Any recompense you can imagine, anything you would ask of me, I would be happy to provide. I’m at your service. Always, Danika.  And it is my most sincere wish that someday, perhaps over time, you might consider being my friend again.</i>
    </b>
  </blockquote>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>Damn that ending. Damn it!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394665176ra/8885767.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now if you'll excuse me, my sleep deprived ass will diving into book 3, which I've been told has some major groveling. And you all know how much I love me a good grovel. And I thank you<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394401485ra/8848466.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436206i/881587.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12284520608192504090"><b>INTENSE!!!!</b><br/><br/><b>Danika </b> and <b>Tristan</b> are struggling to keep their relationship together as their worlds spiral out of control. Tristan is getting messed up with drugs and alcohol and Danika is fighting her tendencies to be an enabler. <br/><br/>Two songs kept cycling through my mind as I was immersed in this love story:<br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=uelHwf8o7_U<br%20/>' rel='nofollow noopener'>Love The Way You Lie</a> by Enimen<br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kAorciL41mc' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Monster</a> by Enimen<br/><br/><b><u>TRISTAN!!!</u> </b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391064968ra/8326077.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>DANIKA!!!</u>
</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391061838ra/8325553.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>March 11th seems so far away. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16139641.Grounded__Up_in_the_Air___3_' title='Grounded (Up in the Air, #3) by R.K. Lilley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Grounded</a> gives me some hope as I wait for <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18681461.Lovely_Trigger__Tristan___Danika___3_' title='Lovely Trigger (Tristan & Danika, #3) by R.K. Lilley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lovely Trigger</a> because Tristan and Danika have a</span>
  <span id="freeText12284520608192504090" style="display:none"><b>INTENSE!!!!</b><br><br><b>Danika </b> and <b>Tristan</b> are struggling to keep their relationship together as their worlds spiral out of control. Tristan is getting messed up with drugs and alcohol and Danika is fighting her tendencies to be an enabler. <br><br>Two songs kept cycling through my mind as I was immersed in this love story:<br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=uelHwf8o7_U&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">Love The Way You Lie</a> by Enimen<br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kAorciL41mc" rel="nofollow noopener">The Monster</a> by Enimen<br><br><b><u>TRISTAN!!!</u> </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391064968ra/8326077.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>DANIKA!!!</u>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391061838ra/8325553.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>March 11th seems so far away. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16139641.Grounded__Up_in_the_Air___3_" title="Grounded (Up in the Air, #3) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">Grounded</a> gives me some hope as I wait for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18681461.Lovely_Trigger__Tristan___Danika___3_" title="Lovely Trigger (Tristan &amp; Danika, #3) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">Lovely Trigger</a> because Tristan and Danika have a conversation that contain all three titles. <blockquote>
<i>"I'm nothing without it and you were my <u>lovely trigger</u> for me. (...) I knew if you looked at me again, I'd hit <u>rock bottom</u>, and this time I wouldn't come back from it.</i> <b>-Tristan</b><br>(...)<br><i>"No, <u>bad things</u> happen when we get together, Tristan." </i><b> -Danika </b>
</blockquote>*********************************************************<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/105659-tristan-danika" rel="nofollow noopener">Tristan &amp; Danika series</a> is interconnected with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/90780-up-in-the-air" rel="nofollow noopener">Up in the Air series</a>. Each series can be read as a standalone series. <br><br>Timeline between the two series:<br><b>{#1 T&amp;A}</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17377032.Bad_Things__Tristan___Danika___1_" title="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. <span id="freeTextContainer18211637982930028400"><b>5 <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395017542ra/8936083.gif' width='40' height='30' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”My hold on him became weaker and weaker, and eventually, every finger broken, my hands opened, and I let him go.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395017321ra/8936037.gif' width='375' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Call me a sucker for heartbreak, but I liked this book SO much better than the first! Perhaps it was the author’s ability to truly rip Danika, Tristan and my heart out slowly page by page in this second installment.<br/><br/>The first book was complete chaos and total drama for me and I had a hard time being invested in Tristan because I had an underlying feeling that he would in f</span>
  <span id="freeText18211637982930028400" style="display:none"><b>5 <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395017542ra/8936083.gif" width="40" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”My hold on him became weaker and weaker, and eventually, every finger broken, my hands opened, and I let him go.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395017321ra/8936037.gif" width="375" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Call me a sucker for heartbreak, but I liked this book SO much better than the first! Perhaps it was the author’s ability to truly rip Danika, Tristan and my heart out slowly page by page in this second installment.<br><br>The first book was complete chaos and total drama for me and I had a hard time being invested in Tristan because I had an underlying feeling that he would in fact betray or destroy Danika. I wasn’t swooning over him, but I did enjoy their chemistry together and in this second book the chemistry was still off the charts but life throws this couple <b>PAIN</b> in the form of one hurdle after another and I truly felt that the author brought it in this book.<br><br><b>
  <i>”What do you want from me?” His voice, at least, was animated now. <br> “Everything!” I shouted, enraged, heartbroken. <br>“Everything you promised, and everything I need. What I’m willing to give to you is what I want from you.”</i>
</b><br><br>Old characters are just as despicable and evil, while new ones were better off lost and sadly, our couple hits rock bottom.<br><br>I’m onto the last installment and looking forward to even more growth for both of these characters while holding out hope for an great hea!<br></span>

After the lost of Jared, they both are battling with their emotions. It made them stronger and closer. <br/><br/><b> <i> " Want me to pull your hair and give you a rough ride, sweetheart?   <span id="freeText3711187242969830717" style="display:none"><br><b> "R.K. LILLEY, YOU ARE EXTRAORDINARILY TALENTED!! FIRST CLASS WRITING" </b> <br><br>Tristan and Danika kicks off from Bad Things perfectly. After the lost of Jared, they both are battling with their emotions. Instead, she decided to wait like a fool for him to return.....   <i>Tragedy never took its full chunk out of you right way. It always took a while to hit you head on, and sink in and for something substantial, some hint of the real feeling, the real reaction, to come to the surface, and this loss was not done taking its toll on us.</i>
</b><br><br>I really enjoyed this one, but it was devastating. Tristan and Danika are both still grieving from the loss suffered in Bad Things. Only finding solace in each other, but the world keeps spinning. And, they find themselves drifting, no matter how hard they try to hold on.<br><br>The hits just kept coming for Tristan and Danika.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395148215ra/8953835.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>R.K. Lilley really puts this couple through the ringer - one thing after another. This was heart breaking to experience something so beautiful fall apart. <br><br><b>
  <i>There was an anchor, tied around both of his ankles, and it was taking him deep, into black fathomless depths, drowning him slowly but surely. I didn’t tell him that he was dragging me down with him.</i>
</b><br><br>I am an angst whore, so I really enjoyed this one. Looking forward to the next book, this couple deserves some happy!</span>

  <span id="freeText18129191736772548674" style="display:none">This series has gotten me by the throat, It is so awesome, exciting, sad, hot and a lots more adjectives. Tristian &amp; Danika story had a love like no other their connection was off the charts. <br /><br />I love you," I spoke softly into his ear. He gripped me harder. "I can’t ever lose you, Danika. I’m not sure I’d survive it." "You’ve got me. And I’m not going anywhere. Not ever." I meant the words when I said them, but life had other plans for us.<br /><br />Only 1 person was jealous of Tristian &amp; Danika relationship, his so call best friend Dean. Dean did everything to separate the two because he missed the old Tristian and wanted fame over anything. So thats how Tristian &amp; Danika relationship continued to be a train wreck always giving Tristian every part of her not considering what she needed going down an endless rabbit hole. As Tristian started to spiral out of control Danika always responded by asking him "What do you need from me, how can I help you" "What is left from a woman when she has given everything to a man...Nothing" So about time Tristian hit rock bottom it was too late, Danika had lost everything that matter to her, nothing else matter, so she gave up on the only man she loved, she let it all go so she could piece her life back to some normalcy without Tristian... UGLY CRY love this series prepare to read in one setting, prepared to go through the journey this author will take you through!!!<br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer639071047" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6135340292007265907"><b>
  <i>""I love you," I spoke softly into his ear. He gripped me harder. "I can't ever lose you, Danika. I'm not sure I'd survive it." "You've got me. And I'm not going anywhere. Not ever." I meant the words when I said them, but life had other plans for us. I was, by nature, a fighter, and no one could say I didn't fight for us. I'd have given my life for that fight. In fact, I very nearly did."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Wow, this book was intense and highly emotional. I though the angst would kill me. I actually have chest</span>
  <span id="freeText6135340292007265907" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>""I love you," I spoke softly into his ear. He gripped me harder. "I can't ever lose you, Danika. I'm not sure I'd survive it." "You've got me. And I'm not going anywhere. Not ever." I meant the words when I said them, but life had other plans for us. I was, by nature, a fighter, and no one could say I didn't fight for us. I'd have given my life for that fight. In fact, I very nearly did."</i>
</b><br><br>Wow, this book was intense and highly emotional. I though the angst would kill me. I actually have chest pains and I still feel like crying. Oh, how my beloved Tristan has fallen. This book shows how addiction not only destroys you, but the ones you love most, as well. This book contained one tragedy after another. I really didn't know if my heart could take it. I have so many emotions swirling inside of me... hatred for that scum of the earth Dean, sorrow for their unimaginable loss, sadness for all that was destroyed, grief over loved ones lost, aggravation for their lack of communication, piety for Danika, great frustration for Tristan, and heartbreak for them both. I have thought up many plots and scenarios on what could have happened to Danika and Tristan's relationship since I read Grounded and in my wildest imaginings I never came up with what actually happened in the end. That ending was, wow, so tragic, so gut-wrenching, so good. I thought the Up In The Air books were really good and memorable, but this series is so beyond compelling and addictively good that I highly recommend it!<br><br><b>
  <i>"There was an anchor, tied around both of his ankles, and it was taking him deep, into black fathomless depths, drowning him slowly but surely. I didn't tell him that he was dragging me down with him."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385977499i/7268123.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="6135340292007265907" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer895011688" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2020117297718374060">4 ½ Addictive, Frustrating, Heartbreaking stars – Contemporary/Erotic Romance<br/><br/>I both hated and loved this book. I thought I was prepared for the angsty continuation of Tristan and Danika’s love story after <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17377032.Bad_Things__Tristan___Danika___1_' title='Bad Things (Tristan & Danika, #1) by R.K. Lilley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Bad Things</a>, but this still eviscerated me. <i>
  <b>Rock Bottom</b>
</i> was emotional, intense, devastating, gut-wrenching, exasperating, and extremely melodramatic, but I was enthralled by their passionate, all-consuming, tumultuous, addictive, and tragic romance and couldn’t swipe my finger across the scr</span>
  <span id="freeText2020117297718374060" style="display:none">4 ½ Addictive, Frustrating, Heartbreaking stars – Contemporary/Erotic Romance<br /><br />I both hated and loved this book. I thought I was prepared for the angsty continuation of Tristan and Danika’s love story after <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17377032.Bad_Things__Tristan___Danika___1_" title="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">Bad Things</a>, but this still eviscerated me. <i>
  <b>Rock Bottom</b>
</i> was emotional, intense, devastating, gut-wrenching, exasperating, and extremely melodramatic, but I was enthralled by their passionate, all-consuming, tumultuous, addictive, and tragic romance and couldn’t swipe my finger across the screen fast enough. <br /><br />So many times I wanted to scream my frustration over their repeatedly bad, destructive choices and actions and the lack of communication and misunderstandings that caused so much needless pain, suffering, misery, and heartbreak. After so much anguish and tragedy...everything these two have gone through together and done to each other, I honestly don’t know how they could possibly ever find their HEA. But I’m already reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18681461.Lovely_Trigger__Tristan___Danika___3_" title="Lovely Trigger (Tristan &amp; Danika, #3) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">Lovely Trigger</a> to find out!<br /><br />Some things that really upset/frustrated/gutted me:<br /><br />**********Spoilers and venting ahead**********<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />Why didn’t Tristan tell Danika that he fought with Dean over him threatening to revenge f*ck her like he did Natalie/Twatalie so that she’d know he was upset on her behalf, not because he was jealous or still had feelings for Twatalie?<br /><br />Why didn’t Danika tell Tristan about Dean’s repeated, nasty comments and threats?<br /><br />Why didn’t Danika tell Jerry, Bev, and/or Tristan about being roughed up and threatened with extortion and rape by the psycho guy at her mom’s trailer? And why did she keep denying anything had happened even after Tristan saw her covered in bruises. Just stupid. Yes, Tristan has a serious anger management issue and caveman temper, but she still could have handled the whole thing so much better and found a way to tell him with Jerry and Bev there to help keep him calm. <br /><br />Why wasn’t Danika more open and honest about her insecurities and fears of infidelity and of them growing apart due to their separation and the temptations of life in LA? <br /><br />Why didn’t Danika tell Tristan about Dean’s twisted plan to set him up, unwitting and unconscious, with Twatalie so that he could see for himself how truly sick and evil Dean had become?<br /><br />And all the tragic stuff that happened because of Tristan’s addiction and in the end that was mostly left unresolved?!?!? Why didn’t they f*cking talk about it?!?!? It’s driving me crazy that Tristan doesn’t know about everything that happened or realize the extent of Danika’s suffering!<br /><br />*The letter that Danika wrote to Tristan telling him to choose rehab or divorce that he seems to know nothing about, instead thinking she just sent him divorce papers.<br />*Tristan's awful, callous actions when she showed up at his house to tell him about the baby and that she wanted to reconcile.<br />*Dean’s assault/threat on Danika in the car before the crash.<br />*All the horrific details of the accident: Danika losing the baby and not being able to have more kids, the surgeries, the extent of her leg injury and required therapy, and that she has a limp and will never dance again. <br />*Danika’s sister, Dahlia, revealing that Dean drugged/raped her and that he’s the father of her baby.<br /><br />I <i>really</i> hope all this sh*t comes out in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18681461.Lovely_Trigger__Tristan___Danika___3_" title="Lovely Trigger (Tristan &amp; Danika, #3) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">Lovely Trigger</a> and that Tristan learns the truth about everything. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Okay, I must read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18681461.Lovely_Trigger__Tristan___Danika___3_" title="Lovely Trigger (Tristan &amp; Danika, #3) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">Lovely Trigger</a> faster!<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_639086361" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639086361" />
    <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read"><img alt="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504717217p2/3068938.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/639086361?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read">Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=i-m-broken">i-m-broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer639086361" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer972579230118001130">This book.....THIS FUCKING BOOK!!! <br/><br/>See the thing is, you know what's coming. It's out there....waiting for you. You're heading for it no matter what. You don't know when. You don't know where. You don't know how. But it's there....patiently waiting for you to arrive......and then it blows your heart and soul up into tiny little pieces.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395021051ra/8936550.gif' width='480' height='284' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>"I was, by nature, a fighter, and no one could say I didn't fight for us. I'd have given my life for that fight. In fact, I very nearly did."</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>In agonizing slow </span>
  <span id="freeText972579230118001130" style="display:none">This book.....THIS FUCKING BOOK!!! <br><br>See the thing is, you know what's coming. It's out there....waiting for you. You're heading for it no matter what. You don't know when. You don't know where. You don't know how. But it's there....patiently waiting for you to arrive......and then it blows your heart and soul up into tiny little pieces.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395021051ra/8936550.gif" width="480" height="284" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"I was, by nature, a fighter, and no one could say I didn't fight for us. I'd have given my life for that fight. In fact, I very nearly did."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>In agonizing slow motion, you watch addiction consume Tristan. Little by little, day in and day out, he loses a little piece of himself while trying desperately to hold onto the one thing that can actually save him. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"She was the one. If I'd ever had a doubt, I didn't now. She was the one I'd be thinking about, longing for, until I took my last breath. If I lost her tomorrow, I'd pine for her like a lovesick fool. This was the kind of love that only hit you once in your life."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>What do you do when the one person you love the most is slowly disappearing right in front of you? When you scratch and claw with every ounce of fight you have to try and save them? Only to find out in the end, that you're not helping at all. There's nothing you can do. And somehow during this epic war, you've begun to lose yourself. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395021051ra/8936551.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>By the end, it's not a question of love, or endurance or even faith.....but of survival. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384886372ra/7010785.gif" width="500" height="282" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"My hold on him became weaker and weaker, and eventually, every finger broken, my hands opened, and I let him go. No one could say I didn't fight for him. No one could say I didn't lose."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>There really aren't any words I can come up with to showcase the rollercoaster of emotions you go through during the last 25-30% of this book. It will make you cry, it will leave you gasping and oddly enough, it will have you hoping. Hoping that the storm has passed, the destruction complete and that, maybe, it was time to clean up and rebuild again. </span>
  <a data-text-id="972579230118001130" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385519768i/7165905.jpg' alt=' photo 34050172-e9ce-4172-a7e9-792edbd7f876.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>So book 2 for Tristan and Danika continues to be an intense emotional roller coaster! Up until about 75% they're relationship is on track. They are together and continue to be in love & explosively hot together! My favorite parts of the book are of course all the Tritan sexy time! He is just yummy!!! If you have read the previous books in this story you know something bad is coming. I hated it, but know it is part of their story. Tristan has su</span>
  <span id="freeText17981209200256023673" style="display:none">(BR with Sharon is an emotional book junkie)<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/aa48baf7-fc6b-4101-9499-0263f053f1ec.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385519768i/7165904.jpg" alt=" photo aa48baf7-fc6b-4101-9499-0263f053f1ec.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/34050172-e9ce-4172-a7e9-792edbd7f876.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385519768i/7165905.jpg" alt=" photo 34050172-e9ce-4172-a7e9-792edbd7f876.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So book 2 for Tristan and Danika continues to be an intense emotional roller coaster! Up until about 75% they're relationship is on track. They are together and continue to be in love &amp; explosively hot together! My favorite parts of the book are of course all the Tritan sexy time! He is just yummy!!! If you have read the previous books in this story you know something bad is coming. I hated it, but know it is part of their story. Tristan has suffered so much loss and turned to his addictions to try to forget. Until he can get himself together he can never be in a relationship with anyone. He really needs rehab and to change his whole lifestyle. I am hoping in book 3 he gets his act together, and wins Danika back. I feel he really needs to work for her forgiveness and trust, and that their love was real and will win out in the end. I look forward to a HEA for them.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/271cc8a7-6235-4f00-a4f0-bda7701365ee.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385592330i/7181550.jpg" alt=" photo 271cc8a7-6235-4f00-a4f0-bda7701365ee.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/64c80769-73db-4f42-a6b4-0995ebb5c902.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394809927i/8909444.jpg" alt=" photo 64c80769-73db-4f42-a6b4-0995ebb5c902.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-She was the one. If I'd ever had a doubt, I didn't now. She was the one I'd be thinking about, longing for, until I took my last breath. If I lost her tomorrow, I'd pine for her like a lovesick fool. This was the kind of love that only hit you once in your life.<br><br>-His eyes shut tightly, and his lips sought out mine, seeking comfort through touch. I gave it to him. I was ready and willing to give him absolutely everything.<br><br>-His hands were reverent, worshipful, devoted, loving; magic.<br><br>-This girl made love like she danced. It was hypnotic. Intoxicating.<br><br>-You're the only one I've felt like this with, and it's the most exciting feeling in the world.<br><br>-This is forever for me, sweetheart. I want it all with you.<br><br>-Having this man love me like he did had become my whole world.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/07dfaad8-4d48-4c55-af56-63c7622a38fe.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385592330i/7181551.jpg" alt=" photo 07dfaad8-4d48-4c55-af56-63c7622a38fe.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('S4kafz81vep1c9FMT+2FLtyv+rSG06SCyFKEYHBfMaH7+tiwAPlEO4ovEsulF9XTntEM3ur8WiGYBqjmjMybmA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('SQZ/9ajoniK6BoD7VrcY8A46NPon2i5eAybvWxSbjef5db06lyRn80VaQ3y8TUgNTETCkEv10P1TcsPd6Agn3g==')})
  }
//]]>

She was forced to see, in the most brutal of ways, that love does not conquer all. Bruised, bloody, and broken she had to walk away. THE AFTERMATH Picking up the pieces of your life after a tragedy is a daunting prospect, and that’s considering you still own all of the pieces. But what if you don’t? What if someone else owns those pieces, and those pieces are a part of your soul? You dig deep and work with what you’ve got. That’s what Danika told herself and believed, every single day, for years. Tristan and Danika’s love had failed every test that life had thrown at them. She couldn’t forget that, not for one second. And if those tests had been overly harsh, well, she wasn’t one to wallow in self-pity. The failure was the thing she had to focus on. The failure was the lesson. She had no intention of working so hard to make it out of hell without learning that lesson well. THE REUNION Over six years after the night that changed everything, Danika finds herself forced to spend the weekend constantly in Tristan’s company, as they attend the wedding of two of their dearest friends. It’s been long enough that she feels they can be friendly again without it destroying her peace of mind, but just a small amount of time in his presence has her remembering something she had forced herself to forget: There’d been a reason she’d gone through hell with this man, for this man, some true good to precede the bad. She shocks herself by quickly giving in to a hunger that she never imagined could still consume her. Even the best intentioned denial has a breaking point. THE HARSH REALITY After everything that’s happened, the rise and the fall, the pain and the aftermath, can these two navigate the waters of acute regret, survive the trials of coming face to face with all that they have lost, and find the strength to try again?
